if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_16();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '5df37173a3bd2369b046ffaa70f2505ea789fd4d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '5df37173a3bd2369b046ffaa70f2505ea789fd4d') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'f6f239029dfcda06a97261c4de2bd7adc5ae290c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_16();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '5df37173a3bd2369b046ffaa70f2505ea789fd4d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('action.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: action.php');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('action.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): action.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('action.php') != 'bf7bfb604c556b0e88bb7be15b869e6ef4d6739d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): action.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('action.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of action.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== 'bf7bfb604c556b0e88bb7be15b869e6ef4d6739d') {
		if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== 'a536d05d99ee2fa16ff8240f9982789184c7b624') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: action.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('action.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('action.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('action.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== 'bf7bfb604c556b0e88bb7be15b869e6ef4d6739d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): action.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
	writefile_19();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php') != '38616dc2587b9e562b8663dfd3f053248dc516c7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php') !== '38616dc2587b9e562b8663dfd3f053248dc516c7') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php') !== '78824c2267bcd11799fef3bafe5d82ec09408823') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_19();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php') !== '38616dc2587b9e562b8663dfd3f053248dc516c7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	writefile_25();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') != '2d9add941515f648bcad7e89b29044e8c402db56') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== '2d9add941515f648bcad7e89b29044e8c402db56') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== 'f81f48b4959dac9a9dc8d5948c82a77f31d9b6e2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_25();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== '2d9add941515f648bcad7e89b29044e8c402db56') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
		}
	}
}
